EAG_wars = {
	EAG_war_on_kent = {
		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 7
		remove_effect = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KNT
				type = annex_everything
			}	
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = ESS
			}
			country_exists = KNT
			EAG = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_seeds_of_wisdom
						has_completed_focus = EAG_communal_mutual_aid
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_seeds_of_wisdom
						has_completed_focus = EAG_army_of_the_people
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_communal_mutual_aid
						has_completed_focus = EAG_army_of_the_people
					}
					#
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_ensuring_our_place_in_heaven
						has_completed_focus = EAG_farmers_self_governance
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_the_main_business
						has_completed_focus = EAG_farmers_self_governance
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_ensuring_our_place_in_heaven
						has_completed_focus = EAG_the_main_business
					}
					#
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_peacemaker
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_are_the_machine
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_walk_in_line
						has_completed_focus = EAG_peacemaker
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_are_the_machine
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_walk_in_line
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

    EAG_project_01_voting = {                           
        allowed = { 
			tag = EAG 
		}
        available = {      
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = false
			}
        }
        activation = {   
			always = false
        }
        is_good = yes                      
        days_mission_timeout = 100              
        timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					EAG_gunzel_count_influence_all = yes
					check_variable = { EAG_our_influence_level > EAG_total_influence_level }
				}
				add_political_power = 50
				set_variable = { EAG_our_influence_level = 0 }
				EAG = {
					country_event = {
						days = 0
						id = EAG_event.90
					}
					country_event = {
						days = 60
						id = EAG_event.68
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					EAG_gunzel_count_influence_all = yes
					check_variable = { EAG_our_influence_level < EAG_total_influence_level }
				}				
				add_political_power = -50   
				set_variable = { EAG_our_influence_level = 0 }
				EAG = {
					country_event = {
						days = 5
						id = EAG_event.71
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					EAG = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = EAG_voting_east_england_agreed
						}
					}
				}
				EAG = {
					country_event = {
						days = 0
						id = EAG_event.91
					}
				}
			}
			if = {

						}
					}
				}

EAG_london_referendum = {
	EAG_london_referendum_mission = {
		cost = 0
		is_good = no                                        
        days_mission_timeout = 65
		allowed = { tag = EAG }
        available = {                           
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = false
			}
        }
		is_good = yes
		activation = {                          
            KNT = {
				has_completed_focus = KNT_london_referendum	
			}			
        }
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { kent_popularity_london > eag_popularity_london }
				}
				KNT = {
					transfer_state = 1160
				}
				add_stability = -0.1
				add_war_support = -0.15
				add_to_variable = {
					var = volk_dev
					value = -3
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = volk_dev
					min = 0
					max = 25
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = mercs_quality
					value = -2
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = mercs_quality
					min = 0
					max = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { kent_popularity_london < eag_popularity_london }
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = volk_dev
					value = 1
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = volk_dev
					min = 0
					max = 25
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = volk_mood
					value = 2
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = volk_mood
					min = 0
					max = 25
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = mercs_quality
					value = 1
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = mercs_quality
					min = 0
					max = 25
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = mercs_mood
					value = 2
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = mercs_mood
					min = 0
					max = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { kent_popularity_london = eag_popularity_london }
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = KNT_london_referendum_mission
					days = 8
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
        }
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

	EAG_invade_kent = {
		cost = 15
		days_remove = 10
		fire_only_once = yes
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { parliament_seat_array^0 > parliament_seat_array^1 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { EAG_anarchist_mood = 0 }
				subtract_from_variable = { parliament_seat_array^0 = 5 }
				subtract_from_variable = { parliament_seat_array^1 = -5 }
				modify_parliament_seat = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_anarchist_medium_support_lost.tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { parliament_seat_array^1 > parliament_seat_array^0 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { EAG_anarchist_mood = 10 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_anarchist_mood_loss.tt
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = KNT
				type = annex_everything
			}	
		}
		available = {
			check_variable = { parliament_seat_array^0 > 10 }
			country_exists = KNT
			EAG = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_seeds_of_wisdom
						has_completed_focus = EAG_communal_mutual_aid
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_seeds_of_wisdom
						has_completed_focus = EAG_army_of_the_people
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_communal_mutual_aid
						has_completed_focus = EAG_army_of_the_people
					}
					#
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_ensuring_our_place_in_heaven
						has_completed_focus = EAG_farmers_self_governance
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_the_main_business
						has_completed_focus = EAG_farmers_self_governance
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_ensuring_our_place_in_heaven
						has_completed_focus = EAG_the_main_business
					}
					#
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_peacemaker
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_are_the_machine
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_walk_in_line
						has_completed_focus = EAG_peacemaker
					}
					AND = {
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_are_the_machine
						has_completed_focus = EAG_we_walk_in_line
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			check_variable = { parliament_seat_array^0 < 10 }
		}
		visible = {
			country_exists = KNT
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

	EAG_anarchist_collapse = {
		is_good = no                                        
        days_mission_timeout = 75
		allowed = { tag = EAG }
        available = {  
			set_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = 0 }
            add_to_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = parliament_seat_array^0 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = parliament_seat_array^1 }
			divide_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = 10 }		
			check_variable = {
				var = parliament_seat_array^0
				value = EAG_anarchist_support_10
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
        }
		activation = {   
			set_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = 0 }
            add_to_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = parliament_seat_array^0 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = parliament_seat_array^1 }
			divide_temp_variable = { EAG_anarchist_support_10 = 10 }
			check_variable = {
				var = parliament_seat_array^0
				value = EAG_anarchist_support_10
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
			EAG = {
				has_completed_focus = EAG_congress_of_communities
			}
        }
		timeout_effect = {
			EAG = {
				add_political_power = -100
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
        }
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

				EAG = { 
					add_timed_idea = { 
						idea = EAG_rebuilding_sealand 
						days = 365
					}
					add_political_power = -250
				}

	EAG_klumb_make_party_coalition_VOLT = {
	   cost = 50
        remove_effect = {
		}	
		complete_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = EAG_klumb_voting_coalition
				value = klumb_parliament_seat_array^2
			}
			EAG = {
				set_country_flag = EAG_klumb_make_party_coalition_VOLT
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_klumb_voting_need_1.tt
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = EAG_klumb_voting_need_2.tt
			custom_trigger_tooltip = { tooltip = EAG_klumb_voting_need_2.tt }
			hidden_trigger = {
				EAG = {
					has_country_flag = EAG_klumb_interaction_menu_open_VOLT
					has_country_flag = EAG_klumb_interaction_menu_open
					OR = {
						has_active_mission = EAG_klumb_mission_voting_NO
						has_active_mission = EAG_klumb_mission_voting_YES
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_active_mission = EAG_klumb_mission_voting_YES
						}
						EAG = {
							check_variable = {
								var = EAG_VOLT_support_level
								value = 61
								compare = greater_than_or_equals
							}	
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_active_mission = EAG_klumb_mission_voting_NO
						}
						EAG = {
							check_variable = {
								var = EAG_VOLT_support_level
								value = 30
								compare = less_than_or_equals
							}	
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = EAG_klumb_make_party_coalition_VOLT
					}	
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			EAG = {
				has_country_flag = EAG_klumb_interaction_menu_open_VOLT
				has_country_flag = EAG_klumb_interaction_menu_open
				OR = {
					has_active_mission = EAG_klumb_mission_voting_NO
					has_active_mission = EAG_klumb_mission_voting_YES
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

	EAG_election_EPC_move = {    
        allowed = { tag = EAG }                 
        available = {  
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = false
			}		
        }
        visible = {
           EAG = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_whitehouse
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_bushell
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_starmer
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_iсke
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_astley
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_yea
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_bates
				}
			}
        }
        activation = {                          
			EAG = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_whitehouse
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_bushell
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_starmer
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_iсke
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_astley
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_yea
					has_country_flag = EAG_run_as_bates
				}
			}			
        }
		cancel_trigger = {
			EAG = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = EAG_klumb_elections_ended
					has_country_flag = EAG_elections_sabotaged
				}
			}
		}
        is_good = no                                        
        days_mission_timeout = 30        
        timeout_effect = {  
			EAG = {
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_member = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_seats = 2 }
						klumb_modify_parliament_seat = yes
						custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_klumb_party_40
					}
					30 = {
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_member = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_seats = 3 }
						klumb_modify_parliament_seat = yes
						custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_klumb_party_30
					}
					15 = {
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_member = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_seats = 5 }
						klumb_modify_parliament_seat = yes
						custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_klumb_party_15
					}
					10 = {
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_member = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_seats = 7 }
						klumb_modify_parliament_seat = yes
						custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_klumb_party_10
					}
					5 = {
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_member = 1 }
						set_temp_variable = { klumb_temp_seats = 8 }
						klumb_modify_parliament_seat = yes
						custom_effect_tooltip = EAG_klumb_party_5
					}
				}
			}
        }
        complete_effect = {                    
        }
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
    }

	EAG_election_campaign = {
		is_good = yes                                        
        days_mission_timeout = 183
		allowed = { tag = EAG }
        available = {                           
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = false
			}
        }
		is_good = yes
		activation = {  
           has_country_flag = EAG_klumb_elections_started			
        }
		timeout_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = EAG_klumb_elections_started
			set_country_flag = EAG_klumb_elections_ended
			EAG = {
				country_event = {
					days = 0
					id = EAG_event.201
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
        }
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
